Didn't think much of the place at first honestly but definitely my favorite restaurant right now. Literally walk in and they know you and what you want.< /Text>

<Text>Before coming to the store, I have previously met the amazing staff of Jesse Boy in a couple of yelp events. I love their enthusiasm and the pride they take in the food they serve.

Although I love the food and friendly staff, it took me awhile to visit their brick and mortar store. Until that day finally happened and realized that I missed out big time for not coming any sooner.

I had the crispy chicken bites on a bed of jasmine rice with a side of greens. I have tried their vegan fried cauliflower before. It's so good that ordering it is a MUST for me. I already had quite a handful on my plate but it's good that the store lets you take only a half order.

As expected, everything was amazing! It's addicting that I'm planning to revisit soon. Looking forward to say hi again to the magnificent team, Jesse, Jay and Ajay.

This is a teeny tiny store with only a few tables and chairs. < review>
Most notably, would be the Charisma and caring attitude that they have for this place. Ajay and Jesse we're both so kind about answering my questions, and making sure that I fully understood everything that they have to offer as they are getting to know what their customers want. From their humble beginnings in the farmers markets of Encino to their soft opening off of Santa Monica Boulevard in Hollywood, it seems they have hit a streak of delicious Korean inspired eats. I was not disappointed. I love having the ability to add more spice. I really enjoyed the cauliflower, and the chicken was almost too much to handle. I got a side of jasmine rice with the a side salad complete with sesame dressing. To top it off, I got a small side of fries  which were perfectly fried out. They reminded me  of smaller  McDonald's french fries  and steak and shake fries . Beautifully salted as well. Be sure to get the radishes! Vegan and vegetarian options, way to go guys! I will definitely be back.< /review>

< Review>
This place offers a delicious and unique offering on Asian style chicken and cauliflower. The portion sizes are very hearty, and the "Diablo" spicy sauce offers respectable heat along with surprisingly complex flavors. The sandwiches are a great choice, with your chicken/cauliflower paired with torched cheese, radishes, and savory sauce. The french fries are an unexpected addition, and will go over well with anyone who enjoys a thin, salty fry. The aguas frescas changes daily based on available ingredients, but have been a reliable treat almost every time. In the end, the food is fantastic, and very non-corporate, but the real highlight are the folks behind the scenes. The staff and owners are incredibly hospitable, and in our experience have gone above and beyond to ensure great food and an even better experience. Jessie Boy is absolutely worth a trip!<//Review>

<Rating>5< /Rating>< text>
I'd say my first Korean fried chicken experience was most definitely a success thanks totally in part to Jesse Boy!

The location is great just off of Santa Monica Blvd and Vine. It was 7:30pm on a Wednesday night and there were plenty of empty parking spaces available. If you are anything like me the anxiety of trying to find parking in LA can lead me to avoid places with bad parking situations. Luckily Jesse Boy was easy in and easy out.

Next, the service was exceptional. I was greeted quickly and with a smile. That's always nice to see and often more rare these days. I ordered the mini Jesse Boy bowl with spicy fried chicken and was offered a sample of their agua fresca and sat down. I immediately got back up because a sip of that delicious drink was not going to cut it. So I ordered the full size for a reasonable $3. One of the co-owners, Ajay introduced himself to me as well and said that a dollar from my agua fresca was going to be donated to a charity as well.

I sat down and got my food. I knew after the first bite that I had a winning dish. All of the flavors came together perfectly. I will warn you though, the spicy chicken was pretty spicy for me. It's not the hottest thing in the world but for someone who enjoys a little kick, it was hot.

Overall, this place is great from the food to the service and I can't wait to head back and try their chicken sandwich and their fried cauliflower that everyone was raving about!< /text>

I ordered the original flavor Cauliflower to and ate it at the Yoshinoya in the same strip center, since there was no facility for washing up at JBs. Did not enjoy the meal at all! Breading was ok, sticky and okay flavor, aside from still being a bit too spicy for my taste. Just didn't taste good overall... Mightve been different if there was some sort of creamy (non spicy, maybe sweet? ) sauce drizzled on top or a creamy sauce offered. I think that any sauce woulda helped with the overall flavor. Returned to request sauce but was offered soy sauce, um...okayyy. The side of fries was apparently the star, since they overwhelmed the dish in quantity. However, they were pretty flavorless and overcooked since they were so skinny. Needed a thicker cut and way less salt. I did not eat many of the fries and tried to stomach the Cauliflower, but I just ended up discarding it at the bus stop, after consuming 50% cauliflower and 10%of fries. It was still full, practically. Maybe a homeless person found it and ate it... The best par was the pickled radishes that were by request only. They were delicious, I'd even consider purchasing them!
While waiting on my order, I saw chicken tender meals and thought they looked like worth trying. Maybe I'll try them next time and update my rating.<//review>

<Rating>4</Rating>< Review>
I came in for the first time this afternoon and was really pleased with the overall experience. The place is small but it feels relaxed and not at all hectic (like a lot of small restaurants can be if they get crowded). The menu is very basic but that's a good thing, in my opinion. And the aguas frescas are to die for. I had the cantaloupe flavor today but I'll be trying all of them.

As far as the staff goes, everyone I interacted with was very sweet and laid back, and I can tell that they aim to please and that they care about making a good impression with their growing customer base. Jesse Boy will be seeing a lot more of me (and people I know, since I'll definitely be spreading the word)!  ;)<//Review>

<UserId.>110756564250551175991</UserId.><Name>Jenny Lynn< /Name><date>1563131431944< /date>< Rating>
5<//Rating>
< text>
This place is hands down the best (and one of the only) places to get LEGIT plant based burgers in downtown Santa Ana.
Any burger with onion rings in them wins a vote from me!
You can also make them protein style wrapped in lettuce instead of a bun.

***They are also the only place in Santa Ana that has KOMBUCHA ON TAP!!!
They feature local breweries and their staff is always helpful and kind. They really know their menu and are knowledgeable about the alcohol percentages on their taps.
I also love that they have a featured new artist every DTSA artwalk, which fits the vibe of the hood considering they are located in artists village, Santa Ana and they are owned and operated by Santaneros!
Definitely taking all my veggie friends here and making this is a stop when I bar hop at night!< /text>

Omg! Love love love this place. It's new and convient little bar and grill. There food is so amazingly tasty. Asparagas fries- tempura batter...nom nom. Next round burger is so delicious. Mine I didn't get the spicy cheese just regular cheese so it was spicy. But their southwest rolls and short rib burger were a hit with our group. The onion rings yummy! They have more items I want to try. Pastrami and salads. The staff- servers, cooks and female manager were all very friendly and it was a nice atmosphere. It's on the corner so you can see down and actoss broadway street. I highly recommend this place for eating and friendly people. I pray they get lots of bussiness and stay open for years. I am going back again. Reasonable prices. Really great food. Yes you need to go it is worth it.</text>

<review>Walked in for dinner on a Sunday night at 1040pm when they close at 12am. I was told that last call for food and drink was at 1130pm. Was seated at 1045pm and placed my order around 1050 which gave me almost an hour to receive my food and eat. The food not only took 50 minutes to cook but when it was finally brought out at 1140pm, the waiter brought it in to go boxes and said that we had to leave cause they were closing in 20 minutes.

Called manager files complaint and gave it another shot.

Came back and got to the restaurant at 11pm on a Monday. I didn't realize it until after I left that they did not close until 1am. It took almost 20mins for someone to finally acknowledge me at 1120pm. The host was about to seat us then the waiter shook his head saying no. The host then said sorry we stop seating at 1130pm. I said okay well its 1120 so I still have 10 mins. The host then said well I mean we stop serving at 1130pm but we stop seating at 1120pm. So we left very dissatisfied.

Walked in for dinner on a Sunday night at 1040pm when they close at 12am. I was told that last call for food and drink was at 1130pm. Was seated at 1045pm and placed my order around 1050 which gave me almost an hour to receive my food and eat. The food not only took 50 minutes to cook but when it was finally brought out at 1140pm, the waiter brought it in to go boxes and said that we had to leave cause they were closing in 20 minutes.

Called manager files complaint and gave it another shot.

Came back and got to the restaurant at 11pm on a Monday. I didn't realize it until after I left that they did not close until 1am. I said okay well its 1120 so I still have 10 mins. The host then said well I mean we stop serving at 1130pm but we stop seating at 1120pm. So we left very dissatisfied.

I call the manager who then gave us a credit for both occasions and explained that they do not stop serving until 1230 on the weekdays because they dont close till 1am. So clearly the host and waiter were trying to close the place early.<//text>
